--- 帖子 #2511 ---
I've coded an indicator which some of you might find useful trading this method. It basically alerts you when:

The 4H, 30M & 5M are all above the 50 level & when the 1M time frame is below the 20 level for a long trade.

Or

The 4H, 30M & 5M are all below the 50 level & when the 1M time frame is above the 80 level for a long trade.

The indicator works perfectly, However I am looking for someone you could possibly insert a few more lines of code so when the long parameters are met an upwards arrow is shown on the chat and when the short parameters are met a downwards arrow is shown on the chart. I work be extremely grateful if someone could help me with this. I've spent hours trying but do not know enough about programming to be able to achieve this!

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

//| Stochs_4H_30M_5M_1M.mq4

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

#property copyright ""

#property indicator_chart_window

datetime       lastbar;

bool           EmailSent;

extern bool    EmailAlert;

extern bool    SoundON;

extern double  highlimit = 80;

extern double  midlimit = 50;

extern double  lowlimit = 20;

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

//| Custom indicator initialization function                         |

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

int init()

{

//---- indicators

Comment ("Stochastic +/- 80/20 Signal Indicator ON");

//----

return(0);

}

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

//| Custom indicator deinitialization function                       |

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

int deinit()

{

//----

Comment ("");

//----

return(0);

}

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

//| Custom indicator iteration function                              |

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

int start()

{

int    counted_bars=IndicatorCounted();

//----

double main_M1 = iStochastic(NULL,PERIOD_M1,5,1,3,MODE_SMA,0,MODE_MAIN,0);

double signal_M1 = iStochastic(NULL,PERIOD_M1,5,1,3,MODE_SMA,0,MODE_SIGNAL,0);

double main_M5 = iStochastic(NULL,PERIOD_M5,5,1,3,MODE_SMA,0,MODE_MAIN,0);

double signal_M5 = iStochastic(NULL,PERIOD_M5,5,1,3,MODE_SMA,0,MODE_SIGNAL,0);

double main_M30 = iStochastic(NULL,PERIOD_M30,5,1,3,MODE_SMA,0,MODE_MAIN,0);

double signal_M30 = iStochastic(NULL,PERIOD_M30,5,1,3,MODE_SMA,0,MODE_SIGNAL,0);

double main_H4 = iStochastic(NULL,PERIOD_H4,5,1,3,MODE_SMA,0,MODE_MAIN,0);

double signal_H4 = iStochastic(NULL,PERIOD_H4,5,1,3,MODE_SMA,0,MODE_SIGNAL,0);

datetime curbar = Time[0];

if (lastbar != curbar)

{

lastbar = curbar;

if ((main_H4 < midlimit) && (main_M30 < midlimit) && (main_M5 < midlimit) && (main_M1 > highlimit))

if ((signal_H4 < midlimit) && (signal_M30 < midlimit) && (signal_M5 < midlimit) && (signal_M1 > highlimit))

{

Alert ("Short Entry Warning On ",Symbol()," ",Period()," min");

if (EmailAlert && !EmailSent)

{

SendMail("Short","Short Entry Warning On " + (StringConcatenate(Symbol()," ",Period())));

EmailSent = true;

}

if (SoundON == true) PlaySound ("alert2.wav");

}

if ((main_H4 > midlimit) && (main_M30 > midlimit) && (main_M5 > midlimit) && (main_M1 < lowlimit))

if ((signal_H4 > midlimit) && (signal_M30 > midlimit) && (signal_M5 > midlimit) && (signal_M1 < lowlimit))

{

Alert ("Long Entry Warning On ",Symbol()," ",Period()," min");

if (EmailAlert && !EmailSent)

{

SendMail("Long","Long Entry Warning On " + (StringConcatenate(Symbol()," ",Period())));

EmailSent = true;

}

if (SoundON == true) PlaySound ("alert2.wav");

}

}

//----

return(0);

}

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

Hi There,

I quite like the signals I was getting from this sexy stochastic system.

Found it frustrating to find pairs giving signals.

So I built a very simple scanning script that I would like to share with any one who would like to try it out.

It scans 19 pairs from M1 to D1 time frames - all selected by external parameter.

I set the  default to only report for H1 H4 and D1 time frames.

Save this ex4 file under \expert\script folder and restart your meta.

You can now run the scanner script any time you like and it will alert you to the pairs and time frames that are presenting sexy stoch signals.

Hope you enjoy it as much as I do.

It is obviously better running this at London open and New York Open times.  I use stop orders and set SL and TP and forget about it!

I also include my template file if you wish to use it.

See picture for the Alerts you will get.

--- 帖子 #2537 ---
Hi there, I like the sexy system too. I was lucky enough to even chat with boxinglife, the creator of this thread. It's a very simple system, but you must consider price action (candle formation) and support and resistance lines in order to trade this with the odds in your favor. The very first pages of this thraed are all you need to understand the basics. As boxingislife told us, it is better to wait for the perfect set ups and use larger time frames. You can use the 4h or 8H to see the big picture and then trade 15m or 30m with de set ups that match the larger time frame context. Other thing you can do to avoid unnecesary headaches is to set up the stochastics calculations with "close to close price" and never make a trade if there is no cross of the 20-80 levels.

I ony use 2 stochs, the third was optional and it can be set off. Stochs are 5,3,3 red and 15,20,10 blue and this is the 4h for gold. As you can see, the Fast stoch (red) show more relaible behavoir. Hope this help. I will share more of my version but I think I will open a new thread in order to respect the original system and to avoid confussion.

Give to this system a chance, it will teach you a lot about forex, futures and stochs.

--- 帖子 #2538 ---
This is another good example of sexy stochs set ups with the NZDUSD.

I set up the sell limit order on sunday afternoon, My expectation was that fast stoch would cross the slow stoch and make a big correction. As it can be seen, I was right in the price level, but wrong in the tme of the entry. Nevertheless I managed my trade and grabed 60 (or 600, depending if youcount the fractional pips) with the 50% of the position, and after I moved my SL to secured 50 pips (or 500) wiht the rest when I saw price was resting 0.76500 area.

The price reversed and hit the SL. I share the picture I was seen at the moment, so now it can be compare to actual chart and see that the correction happen but next day. And the lesson here is: you can be right in the price level, but wrong in the time. And you can be right in the time but wrong in the price level. But with good trade managment and a bit of luck, you can graab some pips. By the time the correction happend I was worry about my mistake and I let the down swing go. This happens a lot, but it is the bred and butter of trading forex.

Hope this help
